<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="499" data-file-width="413" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg/99px-Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg/149px-Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a7/Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg/199px-Bertram_Brockhouse.jpg 2x" width="99"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/Bertram_Brockhouse" title="Bertram Brockhouse">Bertram Brockhouse</a> <span class="noexcerpt" style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Canada" title="Order of Canada">CC</a> <a href="/wiki/Fellow_of_the_Royal_Society_of_Canada" title="Fellow of the Royal Society of Canada">FRSC</a> <a href="/wiki/Fellow_of_the_Royal_Society" title="Fellow of the Royal Society">FRS</a></span>, BA 1947, Nobel Laureate in Physics
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1940" data-file-width="1328" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg/82px-George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg/123px-George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bb/George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg/164px-George_Michael_Volkoff.jpg 2x" width="82"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/George_Volkoff" title="George Volkoff">George Volkoff</a> <span class="noexcerpt" style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Canada" title="Order of Canada">OC</a> <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Order of the British Empire">MBE</a> <a href="/wiki/Fellow_of_the_Royal_Society_of_Canada" title="Fellow of the Royal Society of Canada">FRSC</a></span>, MA 1936, predicted existence of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Neutron_stars" title="Neutron stars">neutron stars</a> and collaborator of <a href="/wiki/J._Robert_Oppenheimer" title="J. Robert Oppenheimer">J. Robert Oppenheimer</a>
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="2288" data-file-width="1283" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg/67px-Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg/101px-Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg/134px-Scylla-_a_book_of_the_dead.jpg 2x" width="67"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/William_Gibson" title="William Gibson">William Gibson</a>, BA 1977, author of <a href="/wiki/Neuromancer" title="Neuromancer">Neuromancer</a>, important figure in the <a href="/wiki/Cyberpunk" title="Cyberpunk">Cyberpunk</a> literary movement
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="800" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg/120px-Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg/180px-Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg/240px-Jeff_Wall_in_2014.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/Jeff_Wall" title="Jeff Wall">Jeff Wall</a> <span class="noexcerpt" style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Canada" title="Order of Canada">OC</a> <a href="/wiki/Fellow_of_the_Royal_Society_of_Canada" title="Fellow of the Royal Society of Canada">FRSC</a></span>, MA 1970, prominent Canadian artist, and most prominent figure of the <a href="/wiki/Vancouver_School" title="Vancouver School">Vancouver School</a>
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="754" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg/88px-Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg/132px-Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg/177px-Right_Livelihood_Award_2009-press_conference-6.jpg 2x" width="88"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/David_Suzuki" title="David Suzuki">David Suzuki</a> <span class="noexcerpt" style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Order_of_Canada" title="Order of Canada">CC</a> <a href="/wiki/Order_of_British_Columbia" title="Order of British Columbia">OBC</a></span> , Professor Emeritus of Genetics. Influential academic, broadcaster, and environmentalist.
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Beverley_McLachlin_(crop).jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="1737" data-file-width="1541" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Beverley_McLachlin_%28crop%29.jpg/106px-Beverley_McLachlin_%28crop%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Beverley_McLachlin_%28crop%29.jpg/160px-Beverley_McLachlin_%28crop%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Beverley_McLachlin_%28crop%29.jpg/213px-Beverley_McLachlin_%28crop%29.jpg 2x" width="106"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/Beverley_McLachlin" title="Beverley McLachlin">Beverley McLachlin</a> <span class="noexcerpt" style="font-size:85%;"><a href="/wiki/Queen%27s_Privy_Council_for_Canada" title="Queen's Privy Council for Canada">PC</a></span>, 17th <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_Chief_Justices_of_the_Supreme_Court_of_Canada" title="List of Chief Justices of the Supreme Court of Canada">Chief Justice</a> of Canada.
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px"><div style="width: 155px">
<div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;"><div style="margin:15px auto;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg"><img alt="" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="388" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg/97px-Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg/145px-Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg/194px-Bjarni_Tryggvason.jpg 2x" width="97"/></a></div></div>
<div class="gallerytext">
<p><a href="/wiki/Bjarni_Tryggvason" title="Bjarni Tryggvason">Bjarni Tryggvason</a> B.ASc 1972, Icelandic-Canadian astronaut and academic who participated in <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> mission <a href="/wiki/STS-85" title="STS-85">STS-85</a>.
</p>
</div>
</div></li>
</ul>
<p>Throughout UBC's history, faculty, alumni, and former students have played prominent roles in many different fields. Many UBC alumni and faculty have gone on to win awards including seven <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nobel_Prizes" title="Nobel Prizes">Nobel Prizes</a> and 67 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rhodes_Scholarships" title="Rhodes Scholarships">Rhodes Scholarships</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-facts1_9-2"><a href="#cite_note-facts1-9">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup>
</p><p>Former alumni have won Nobel Prizes: <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mundell" title="Robert Mundell">Robert Mundell</a> (Economic Sciences) who graduated from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UBC_Department_of_Economics" title="UBC Department of Economics">UBC Department of Economics</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bertram_Brockhouse" title="Bertram Brockhouse">Bertram Brockhouse</a> (Physics).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup> Five former faculty members of the UBC have also received a Nobel Prize: <a href="/wiki/Michael_Smith_(chemist)" title="Michael Smith (chemist)">Michael Smith</a> (Chemistry), <a href="/wiki/Har_Gobind_Khorana" title="Har Gobind Khorana">Har Gobind Khorana</a> (Physiology or Medicine), <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Kahneman" title="Daniel Kahneman">Daniel Kahneman</a> (Economics), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hans_G._Dehmelt" title="Hans G. Dehmelt">Hans G. Dehmelt</a> (Physics), and <a href="/wiki/Carl_Wieman" title="Carl Wieman">Carl Wieman</a> (Physics).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup>
</p><p>Many former students have gained local and national prominence in government. The university has produced three Canadian Prime Ministers: <a href="/wiki/John_Turner" title="John Turner">John Turner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kim_Campbell" title="Kim Campbell">Kim Campbell</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Justin_Trudeau" title="Justin Trudeau">Justin Trudeau</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup> The leader of the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Canada" title="Liberal Party of Canada">Liberal Party of Canada</a>, Member of Parliament and the 23rd Prime Minister of Canada <a href="/wiki/Justin_Trudeau" title="Justin Trudeau">Justin Trudeau</a> completed his BEd. at UBC in 1998.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup> Canadian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Joe_Clark" title="Joe Clark">Joe Clark</a> briefly attended UBC law.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/George_Stanley" title="George Stanley">George Stanley</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_Governor_of_New_Brunswick" title="Lieutenant Governor of New Brunswick">Lieutenant Governor of New Brunswick</a> and creator of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadian_flag" title="Canadian flag">Canadian flag</a> had also served as faculty.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup> Alumni <a href="/wiki/Mike_Harcourt" title="Mike Harcourt">Mike Harcourt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Glen_Clark" title="Glen Clark">Glen Clark</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ujjal_Dosanjh" title="Ujjal Dosanjh">Ujjal Dosanjh</a> have been Premiers of British Columbia:,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup> People of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/University_of_British_Columbia_Faculty_of_Law" title="University of British Columbia Faculty of Law">UBC Law</a> have also served on the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Canada" title="Supreme Court of Canada">Supreme Court of Canada</a>: former faculty member <a href="/wiki/Beverley_McLachlin" title="Beverley McLachlin">Beverley McLachlin</a> and alumnus <a href="/wiki/Frank_Iacobucci" title="Frank Iacobucci">Frank Iacobucci</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup> Other examples are
</p>
<ul><li>Canadian academic, science broadcaster and environmental activist <a href="/wiki/David_Suzuki" title="David Suzuki">David Suzuki</a> was a professor in UBC's genetics department from 1963 until his retirement in 2001.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joel_Bakan" title="Joel Bakan">Joel Bakan</a>, author of <a href="/wiki/The_Corporation_(2003_film)" title="The Corporation (2003 film)">The Corporation: The Pathological Pursuit of Profit and Power</a> is a professor at the faculty of law.</li>
<li>Psychologist <a href="/wiki/Albert_Bandura" title="Albert Bandura">Albert Bandura</a> is an alumnus of UBC.</li>
<li>Actress <a href="/wiki/Evangeline_Lilly" title="Evangeline Lilly">Evangeline Lilly</a> attended UBC and earned her degree in International Relations.</li>
<li>Singer/songwriter <a href="/wiki/Dan_Mangan" title="Dan Mangan">Dan Mangan</a> attended UBC, earning a BA in English Literature.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup></li>
<li>Author and historian <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Berton" title="Pierre Berton">Pierre Berton</a> majored in history at UBC.</li>
<li>Man-in-Motion <a href="/wiki/Rick_Hansen" title="Rick Hansen">Rick Hansen</a> was the first student with a physical disability to graduate in <a href="/wiki/Physical_education" title="Physical education">physical education</a> from UBC.</li>
<li>Opera singers <a href="/wiki/Judith_Forst" title="Judith Forst">Judith Forst</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ben_Heppner" title="Ben Heppner">Ben Heppner</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lance_Ryan" title="Lance Ryan">Lance Ryan</a> studied music at UBC.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_Cheriton" title="David Cheriton">David Cheriton</a>, who graduated from UBC in 1973 is a <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> founding investor and computer science professor at <a href="/wiki/Stanford_University" title="Stanford University">Stanford University</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup></li>
<li>Science fiction writer <a href="/wiki/William_Gibson" title="William Gibson">William Gibson</a>, who coined the term "<a href="/wiki/Cyberspace" title="Cyberspace">cyberspace</a>", earned his bachelor's degree in English at UBC.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup></li></ul>
<p>UBC alumni have also held important positions in the academia. Notable examples are: 
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Indira_Samarasekera" title="Indira Samarasekera">Indira Samarasekera</a>, twelfth president of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Alberta" title="University of Alberta">University of Alberta</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amit_Chakma" title="Amit Chakma">Amit Chakma</a>, president of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Western_Ontario" title="University of Western Ontario">University of Western Ontario</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Muriel_Kennett_Wales" title="Muriel Kennett Wales">Muriel Kennett Wales</a>, believed to have been the first Irish-born woman to earn a PhD in pure mathematics.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/John_H._McArthur" title="John H. McArthur">John H. McArthur</a>, dean emeritus of the <a href="/wiki/Harvard_Business_School" title="Harvard Business School">Harvard Business School</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thomas_Franck_(lawyer)" title="Thomas Franck (lawyer)">Thomas Franck (lawyer)</a>, who was the Murry and Ida Becker Professor of Law at <a href="/wiki/New_York_University" title="New York University">New York University</a> and former Editor-in-Chief of the <a href="/wiki/American_Journal_of_International_Law" title="American Journal of International Law">American Journal of International Law</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/David_H._Turpin" title="David H. Turpin">David H. Turpin</a>, sixth president of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Victoria" title="University of Victoria">University of Victoria</a> and thirteenth president of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Alberta" title="University of Alberta">University of Alberta</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nemkumar_Banthia" title="Nemkumar Banthia">Nemkumar Banthia</a>, a fellow of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Society_of_Canada" title="Royal Society of Canada">Royal Society of Canada</a> and CEO of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=IC-IMPACTS&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="IC-IMPACTS (page does not exist)">IC-IMPACTS</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Michiel_Horn" title="Michiel Horn">Michiel Horn</a>, member of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Society_of_Canada" title="Royal Society of Canada">Royal Society of Canada</a> and professor emeritus of history at <a href="/wiki/York_University" title="York University">York University</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Monica_Lam" title="Monica Lam">Monica Lam</a>, a computer science professor at <a href="/wiki/Stanford_University" title="Stanford University">Stanford University</a> and founder of <a href="/wiki/Moka5" title="Moka5">Moka5</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176"><a href="#cite_note-176">[176]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Frank_Iacobucci" title="Frank Iacobucci">Frank Iacobucci</a>, a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puisne_Justice" title="Puisne Justice">Puisne Justice</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Canada" title="Supreme Court of Canada">Supreme Court of Canada</a></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Further_reading">Further reading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=University_of_British_Columbia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Further reading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>William A. Bruneau, <i>A Matter of Identities: A History of the UBC Faculty Association, 1920–1990</i>. Vancouver: University of British Columbia Faculty Association, 1990.</li>
<li><cite class="citation journal">Bruneau, William A. (1994). "Toward a New Collective Biography: The University of British Columbia Professoriate, 1915–1945". <i>Canadian Journal of Education</i>. <b>19</b> (1): 65–79. <a href="/wiki/JSTOR" title="JSTOR">JSTOR</a> <a class="external text" href="//www.jstor.org/stable/1495307" rel="nofollow">1495307</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Canadian+Journal+of+Education&amp;rft.atitle=Toward+a+New+Collective+Biography%3A+The+University+of+British+Columbia+Professoriate%2C+1915%E2%80%931945&amp;rft.volume=19&amp;rft.issue=1&amp;rft.pages=65-79&amp;rft.date=1994&amp;rft_id=%2F%2Fwww.jstor.org%2Fstable%2F1495307&amp;rft.aulast=Bruneau&amp;rft.aufirst=William+A.&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AUniversity+of+British+Columbia"></span><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/></li>
<li>Eric Damer and Herbert Rosengarten. <i>UBC: The First 100 Years.</i> Vancouver: Friesens, 2009.</li>
<li>Michiel Horn."Under the Gaze of George Vancouver: The University of British Columbia and the Provincial Government, 1913–1939." BC Studies 83 (Autumn 1989).</li>
<li>William C. Gibson <i>Wesbrook &amp; His University</i> (Vancouver: University of British Columbia Press)</li>
<li>Sheldon Goldfarb <i>The Hundred-Year Trek: A History of Student Life at UBC.</i> Victoria: Heritage House, 2017.</li>
<li>H.T. Logan, <i>Tuum Est: A History of the University of British Columbia.</i> Vancouver: University of British Columbia, 1958.</li>
<li>Wayne Skene. "UBC: a Portrait." Vancouver: Tribute Books, 2003.</li>
<li>Lee Stewart. <i>"It's Up to You": Women at UBC in the Early Years.</i> Vancouver: University of British Columbia Press, 1990.</li>
